<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Dark Magician Girl</h1>			<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">

<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about the card. For the character, see <a href="/wiki/Dark_Magician_Girl_(character)" title="Dark Magician Girl (character)">Dark Magician Girl (character)</a>. For the archetype, see <a href="/wiki/Dark_Magician_Girl_(archetype)" title="Dark Magician Girl (archetype)">"Dark Magician Girl" (archetype)</a>. For the set, see <a href="/wiki/Dark_Magician_Girl_pack" title="Dark Magician Girl pack">Dark Magician Girl pack</a>.   </div>

  <td><span lang="ko">블랙 매지션 걸</span></td><td rowspan="2"><span lang="ko">①: 이 카드의 공격력은, 서로의 묘지의 "블랙 매지션" "매지션 오브 블랙 카오스"의 수 × 300 올린다.</span>
  </td>

  <td lang="ko-Latn" style="font-style: italic;">Beullaek Maejisyeon Geol</td>

  <th scope="row">Simplified Chinese</th>
  <td><span lang="zh-Hans">黑魔导女孩</span></td><td><span lang="zh-Hans">①：此卡的攻击力，上升相当于双方墓地的“黑魔导”、“黑混沌之魔导”数量×300的数值。</span>
